class \mbox{\hyperlink{classtesseract__planning_1_1SimpleMotionPlanner}{Simple\+Motion\+Planner}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em The simple planner is meant to be a tool for assigning values to the seed. The planner simply loops over all of the Plan\+Instructions and then calls the appropriate function from the profile. These functions do not depend on the seed, so this may be used to initialize the seed appropriately using e.\+g. linear interpolation. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacetesseract__planning_a97a7a198edf46fea10c33898f4b1e2c5}\label{namespacetesseract__planning_a97a7a198edf46fea10c33898f4b1e2c5}} 
\index{tesseract\_planning@{tesseract\_planning}!PlannerProfileRemapping@{PlannerProfileRemapping}}
\index{PlannerProfileRemapping@{PlannerProfileRemapping}!tesseract\_planning@{tesseract\_planning}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{PlannerProfileRemapping}{PlannerProfileRemapping}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily using \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetesseract__planning_a97a7a198edf46fea10c33898f4b1e2c5}{tesseract\+\_\+planning\+::\+Planner\+Profile\+Remapping}} = typedef std\+::unordered\+\_\+map$<$std\+::string, std\+::unordered\+\_\+map$<$std\+::string, std\+::string$>$ $>$}

This used to store planner specific profile mapping with the request

For example say you have a profile named Raster in your command language. Say you have multiple Raster profiles for descartes \{Raster, Raster1, Rester2\}. This allows you to remap the meaning of Raster in the command language to say Raster2 for the specific planner Descartes by Map$<$Descartes, Map$<$\+Raster, Raster1$>$$>$. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacetesseract__planning_ae98ce6e841caa404388d1689b4ffe1db}\label{namespacetesseract__planning_ae98ce6e841caa404388d1689b4ffe1db}} 
\index{tesseract\_planning@{tesseract\_planning}!PoseSamplerFn@{PoseSamplerFn}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{RobotConfig}{RobotConfig}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetesseract__planning_adc15a5456ea446dfa3dc95852bc9d579}{tesseract\+\_\+planning\+::\+Robot\+Config}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}



The Robot\+Config enum. 

The first letter refers to \textquotesingle{}Flip vs No-\/\+Flip\textquotesingle{}, think of the human arm as the robot this would relate to wrist flipped or not flipped.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Which is indicated by flipping the sign of J5 requiring J4 and J6 to move by +/-\/180 degrees The second letter refers to \textquotesingle{}Up vs Down\textquotesingle{} think of the human arm as the robot this would relate to elbow up or down
\item Which is indicated, J3 is greater than or less than 90 degrees and tool0 positiion x is positive or negative The third letter refers to \textquotesingle{}Front vs Back\textquotesingle{} think of the human arm as the robot this would relate to arm in front or back 
\end{DoxyItemize}\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::vector$<$ std\+::reference\+\_\+wrapper$<$ Instruction $>$ $>$ tesseract\+\_\+planning\+::flatten\+Program (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Composite\+Instruction \&}]{composite\+\_\+instruction }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Flattens a Composite\+Instruction into a vector of Instruction\&. 

If /p composite\+\_\+instruction parameter has a start instruction it is added but child composites are not check for start instructions.

\end{DoxyParams}

\index{tesseract\_planning@{tesseract\_planning}!flattenProgramToPattern@{flattenProgramToPattern}}
\index{flattenProgramToPattern@{flattenProgramToPattern}!tesseract\_planning@{tesseract\_planning}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{flattenProgramToPattern()}{flattenProgramToPattern()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::vector$<$ std\+::reference\+\_\+wrapper$<$ Instruction $>$ $>$ tesseract\+\_\+planning\+::flatten\+Program\+To\+Pattern (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Composite\+Instruction \&}]{composite\+\_\+instruction,  }\item[{const Composite\+Instruction \&}]{pattern }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Flattens a composite instruction to the same pattern as the pattern composite instruction. ie, an element of instruction will only be flattened if the corresponding element in pattern is flattenable. 

If /p composite\+\_\+instruction parameter has a start instruction it is added but child composites are not check for start instructions.

The motivation for this utility is a case where you flatten only the elements in a seed that correspond to composites in the parent instruction


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em instruction} & Composite\+Instruction that will be flattened \\
\hline
{\em pattern} & Composite\+Instruction used to determine if instruction will be flattened \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A new flattened vector referencing the original instruction elements 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\em joint\+\_\+values} & The joint values of the robot \\

{\em limits} & The robot joint limits \\
\hline
{\em coupling\+\_\+limits} & Limits for robot joint 4 and 6 coupling. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
True if within limits otherwise false 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{LVSInterpolateStateWaypoint()}{LVSInterpolateStateWaypoint()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Composite\+Instruction tesseract\+\_\+planning\+::\+LVSInterpolate\+State\+Waypoint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Cartesian\+Waypoint \&}]{start,  }\item[{const Cartesian\+Waypoint \&}]{end,  }\item[{const Plan\+Instruction \&}]{base\+\_\+instruction,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structtesseract__planning_1_1PlannerRequest}{Planner\+Request}} \&}]{request,  }\item[{const Manipulator\+Info \&}]{manip\+\_\+info,  }\item[{double}]{state\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length,  }\item[{double}]{translation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length,  }\item[{double}]{rotation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length,  }\item[{int}]{min\+\_\+steps }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



LVSInterpolate\+State\+Waypoint(\+Cartesian\+Waypoint to Cartesian\+Waypoint) 

This function interpolates the motion from start state to end state. Results are stored in State\+Waypoint objects.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the number of steps for the plan will be calculated such that\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the translational distance between successive steps is no longer than translation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment
\item the rotational distance between successive steps is no longer than rotation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment
\item the number of steps for the plan will be calculated such that the norm of all joint distances between successive steps is no longer than state\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length
\item the max steps from the above calculations will be be compared to the min\+\_\+steps and the largest will be chosen
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item the interpolation will be done based on the condition below
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Case 1\+: Joint solution found for start and end cartesian waypoint
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item It interpolates the joint position from the start to the end state
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Case 2\+: Joint solution only found for start cartesian waypoint
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item It creates number states based on the steps and sets the value to found start solution
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Case 3\+: Joint solution only found for end cartesian waypoint
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item It creates number states based on the steps and sets the value to found end solution
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Case 4\+: No joint solution found for end and start cartesian waypoint
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item It creates number states based on the steps and sets the value to the current state of the environment
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em start} & The joint state at the start of the plan \\
\hline
{\em end} & The joint state at the end of the plan \\
\hline
{\em base\+\_\+instruction} & The base plan instruction \\
\hline
{\em request} & The planning request information \\
\hline
{\em manip\+\_\+info} & The manipulator information provided by the parent composite instruction \\
\hline
{\em state\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length} & The maximum joint distance (norm of changes to all joint positions) between successive steps \\
\hline
{\em translation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length} & The maximum translational distance between successive steps \\
\hline
{\em rotation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length} & The maximaum rotational distance between successive steps \\
\hline
{\em min\+\_\+steps} & The minimum number of steps for the plan \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A composite instruction of move instruction with state waypoints 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Todo}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{todo__todo000029}{Todo}}]\+: May be nice to add contact checking to find best solution, but may not be neccessary because this is used to generate the seed. \end{DoxyRefDesc}


\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Todo}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{todo__todo000029}{Todo}}]\+: May be nice to add contact checking to find best solution, but may not be neccessary because this is used to generate the seed. \end{DoxyRefDesc}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{LVSInterpolateStateWaypoint()}{LVSInterpolateStateWaypoint()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Composite\+Instruction tesseract\+\_\+planning\+::\+LVSInterpolate\+State\+Waypoint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Joint\+Waypoint \&}]{start,  }\item[{const Joint\+Waypoint \&}]{end,  }\item[{const Plan\+Instruction \&}]{base\+\_\+instruction,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structtesseract__planning_1_1PlannerRequest}{Planner\+Request}} \&}]{request,  }\item[{const Manipulator\+Info \&}]{manip\+\_\+info,  }\item[{double}]{state\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length,  }\item[{double}]{translation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length,  }\item[{double}]{rotation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length,  }\item[{int}]{min\+\_\+steps }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



LVSInterpolate\+State\+Waypoint(\+Joint\+Waypoint to Joint\+Waypoint) 

This function interpolates the motion from start state to end state. Results are stored in State\+Waypoint objects.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the number of steps for the plan will be calculated such that\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the translational distance between successive steps is no longer than translation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment
\item the rotational distance between successive steps is no longer than rotation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment
\item the number of steps for the plan will be calculated such that the norm of all joint distances between successive steps is no longer than state\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length
\item the max steps from the above calculations will be be compared to the min\+\_\+steps and the largest will be chosen
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item the interpolation will be done in joint space
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em start} & The joint state at the start of the plan \\
\hline
{\em end} & The joint state at the end of the plan \\
\hline
{\em base\+\_\+instruction} & The base plan instruction \\
\hline
{\em request} & The planning request information \\
\hline
{\em manip\+\_\+info} & The manipulator information provided by the parent composite instruction \\
\hline
{\em state\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length} & The maximum joint distance (norm of changes to all joint positions) between successive steps \\
\hline
{\em translation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length} & The maximum translational distance between successive steps \\
\hline
{\em rotation\+\_\+longest\+\_\+valid\+\_\+segment\+\_\+length} & The maximaum rotational distance between successive steps \\
\hline
{\em min\+\_\+steps} & The minimum number of steps for the plan \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A composite instruction of move instruction with state waypoints 
\end{DoxyReturn}
